14.6 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 4: Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… SQLite

SQLite â€” Ğ²ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¾ĞµĞ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ğ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…. ĞĞµ Ñ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°, Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ÑÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğµ.

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» models/db.js:

const Database = require('better-sqlite3');
const path = require('path');

// Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼/Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ñƒ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…
const db = new Database(path.join(__dirname, '..', 'database.sqlite'));

// Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ñ… Ğ½ĞµÑ‚
db.exec(`
    -- ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ğ¸
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        password TEXT NOT NULL,
        name TEXT NOT NULL,
        phone TEXT,
        role TEXT DEFAULT 'user',
        created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
    );

    -- ĞšĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¸
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS categories (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        name TEXT NOT NULL,
        slug TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        description TEXT,
        sort_order INTEGER DEFAULT 0
    );

    -- Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS products (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        name TEXT NOT NULL,
        slug TEXT UNIQUE,
        description TEXT,
        price REAL NOT NULL,
        old_price REAL,
        image TEXT,
        category_id INTEGER,
        stock INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        status TEXT DEFAULT 'active',
        featured INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        FOREIGN KEY (category_id) REFERENCES categories(id)
    );

    -- Ğ—Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ñ‹
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS orders (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        user_id INTEGER,
        name TEXT NOT NULL,
        email TEXT NOT NULL,
        phone TEXT NOT NULL,
        address TEXT NOT NULL,
        comment TEXT,
        total REAL NOT NULL,
        status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
        created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
    );

    -- Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹ Ğ² Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğµ
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS order_items (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        order_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
        product_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
        product_name TEXT NOT NULL,
        price REAL NOT NULL,
        quantity INTEGER NOT NULL,
        FOREIGN KEY (order_id) REFERENCES orders(id),
        FOREIGN KEY (product_id) REFERENCES products(id)
    );

    -- ĞšĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ° (Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…)
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cart (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        user_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
        product_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
        quantity INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
        UNIQUE(user_id, product_id),
        FOREIGN KEY (user_id) REFERENCES users(id),
        FOREIGN KEY (product_id) REFERENCES products(id)
    );
`);

module.exports = db;

14.7 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 5: Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» server.js:

require('dotenv').config();
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const path = require('path');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// ============================================
// MIDDLEWARE (Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶ÑƒÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ‡Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‡Ğ¸ĞºĞ¸)
// ============================================

// Ğ‘ĞµĞ·Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ°ÑĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ: Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ HTTP Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ¸
app.use(helmet({
    contentSecurityPolicy: false  // ĞÑ‚ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸
}));

// CORS: Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ñ€ĞµÑˆĞ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‹ Ñ Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¸Ñ… Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ¾Ğ²
app.use(cors());

// ĞŸĞ°Ñ€ÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³ JSON Ğ² Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ğµ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ°
app.use(express.json());

// Ğ¡Ñ‚Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑĞºĞ¸Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹ (HTML, CSS, JS)
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// Ğ—Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚ Ğ±Ñ€ÑƒÑ‚Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€ÑĞ° (100 Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ² Ğ·Ğ° 15 Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚)
const limiter = rateLimit({
    windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000,
    max: 100,
    message: { error: 'Ğ¡Ğ»Ğ¸ÑˆĞºĞ¾Ğ¼ Ğ¼Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ²' }
});
app.use('/api/', limiter);

// ============================================
// ĞœĞĞ Ğ¨Ğ Ğ£Ğ¢Ğ« API
// ============================================

// ĞŸĞ¾Ğ´ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ñ€Ğ¾ÑƒÑ‚Ñ‹
app.use('/api/products', require('./routes/products'));
app.use('/api/auth', require('./routes/auth'));
app.use('/api/orders', require('./routes/orders'));
app.use('/api/cart', require('./routes/cart'));

// ============================================
// HTML Ğ¡Ğ¢Ğ ĞĞĞ˜Ğ¦Ğ«
// ============================================

// Ğ’ÑĞµ Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‹ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ´Ğ°ÑÑ‚ index.html
app.get('*', (req, res) => {
    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ»Ğ¸ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»
    const filePath = path.join(__dirname, 'public', req.path);
    if (req.path.includes('.')) {
        return res.sendFile(filePath);
    }
    res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

// ============================================
// ĞĞ‘Ğ ĞĞ‘ĞĞ¢ĞšĞ ĞĞ¨Ğ˜Ğ‘ĞĞš
// ============================================

app.use((err, req, res, next) => {
    console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ°:', err);
    res.status(500).json({
        success: false,
        error: 'Ğ’Ğ½ÑƒÑ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ½Ğ½ÑÑ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
    });
});

// ============================================
// Ğ—ĞĞŸĞ£Ğ¡Ğš Ğ¡Ğ•Ğ Ğ’Ğ•Ğ Ğ
// ============================================

app.listen(PORT, () => {
    console.log(`Ğ¡ĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿ÑƒÑ‰ĞµĞ½: http://localhost:${PORT}`);
});

14.8 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 6: Middleware Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

JWT (JSON Web Token) â€” ÑĞ¿Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ± Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ±ĞµĞ· ÑĞµÑÑĞ¸Ğ¹. Ğ¡ĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ñ‚ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğµ, ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞµĞ½Ñ‚ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ñ‚ ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ² ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞµ.

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» middleware/auth.js:

const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const db = require('../models/db');

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-secret-key';

/**
 * ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° JWT Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½Ğ° (Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ)
 */
function authenticate(req, res, next) {
    // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½ Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ° Authorization: Bearer <token>
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;

    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
        return res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ'
        });
    }

    const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];

    try {
        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¸ Ğ´ĞµĞºĞ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½
        const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);

        // ĞĞ°Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ² Ğ‘Ğ”
        const user = db.prepare(
            'SELECT id, email, name, phone, role FROM users WHERE id = ?'
        ).get(decoded.userId);

        if (!user) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½'
            });
        }

        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ² Ğ¾Ğ±ÑŠĞµĞºÑ‚ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ°
        req.user = user;
        next();

    } catch (error) {
        return res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞĞµĞ´ĞµĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½'
        });
    }
}

/**
 * ĞĞ¿Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ (Ğ½Ğµ Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµÑ‚ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½Ğ° Ğ½ĞµÑ‚)
 */
function optionalAuth(req, res, next) {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;

    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
        return next();  // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ±ĞµĞ· Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
    }

    const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];

    try {
        const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
        const user = db.prepare(
            'SELECT id, email, name, phone, role FROM users WHERE id = ?'
        ).get(decoded.userId);

        if (user) {
            req.user = user;
        }
    } catch (error) {
        // Ğ˜Ğ³Ğ½Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾ÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ¸ â€” Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¸Ğ´Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ÑŒÑˆĞµ Ğ±ĞµĞ· Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
    }

    next();
}

/**
 * ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°
 */
function requireAdmin(req, res, next) {
    if (!req.user || req.user.role !== 'admin') {
        return res.status(403).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'Ğ”Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€ĞµÑ‰Ñ‘Ğ½. Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒÑÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ°Ğ²Ğ° Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°.'
        });
    }
    next();
}

/**
 * Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ JWT Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½Ğ°
 */
function createToken(userId) {
    return jwt.sign({ userId }, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '7d' });
}

module.exports = { authenticate, optionalAuth, requireAdmin, createToken };

14.9 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 7: API Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» routes/auth.js:

const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const db = require('../models/db');
const { authenticate, createToken } = require('../middleware/auth');

/**
 * POST /api/auth/register - Ğ ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
 */
router.post('/register', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { email, password, name, phone } = req.body;

        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ
        if (!email || !password || !name) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ'
            });
        }

        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚ Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ
        const existing = db.prepare(
            'SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = ?'
        ).get(email.toLowerCase());

        if (existing) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ñ Ñ‚Ğ°ĞºĞ¸Ğ¼ email ÑƒĞ¶Ğµ ÑÑƒÑ‰ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²ÑƒĞµÑ‚'
            });
        }

        // Ğ¥ĞµÑˆĞ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ (10 Ñ€Ğ°ÑƒĞ½Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ²)
        const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
        const result = db.prepare(`
            INSERT INTO users (email, password, name, phone)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
        `).run(email.toLowerCase(), hashedPassword, name, phone || null);

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½
        const token = createToken(result.lastInsertRowid);

        res.status(201).json({
            success: true,
            data: {
                token,
                user: {
                    id: result.lastInsertRowid,
                    email: email.toLowerCase(),
                    name,
                    phone
                }
            }
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ñ€ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

/**
 * POST /api/auth/login - Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´
 */
router.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { email, password } = req.body;

        // ĞĞ°Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
        const user = db.prepare(
            'SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ?'
        ).get(email.toLowerCase());

        if (!user) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ email Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ'
            });
        }

        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ
        const validPassword = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);

        if (!validPassword) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ email Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ'
            });
        }

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½
        const token = createToken(user.id);

        res.json({
            success: true,
            data: {
                token,
                user: {
                    id: user.id,
                    email: user.email,
                    name: user.name,
                    phone: user.phone,
                    role: user.role
                }
            }
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

/**
 * GET /api/auth/me - ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑƒÑ‰ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ

    res.json({

    });

14.10 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 8: API Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» routes/products.js:

const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const db = require('../models/db');

/**
 * GET /api/products - Ğ¡Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¾Ğº Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²
 */
router.get('/', (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { category, search, page = 1, limit = 20 } = req.query;
        const offset = (page - 1) * limit;

        let sql = `
            SELECT p.*, c.name as category_name
            FROM products p
            LEFT JOIN categories c ON p.category_id = c.id
            WHERE p.status = 'active'
        `;
        const params = [];

        // Ğ¤Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒÑ‚Ñ€ Ğ¿Ğ¾ ĞºĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¸
        if (category) {
            sql += ` AND c.slug = ?`;
            params.push(category);
        }

        // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¸ÑĞº Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ·Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ
        if (search) {
            sql += ` AND p.name LIKE ?`;
            params.push(`%${search}%`);
        }

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ° Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
        sql += ` ORDER BY p.created_at DESC LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`;
        params.push(parseInt(limit), parseInt(offset));

        const products = db.prepare(sql).all(...params);

        // Ğ¡Ñ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾Ğ±Ñ‰ĞµĞµ ĞºĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾
        let countSql = `
            SELECT COUNT(*) as total FROM products p
            LEFT JOIN categories c ON p.category_id = c.id
            WHERE p.status = 'active'
        `;
        const countParams = [];

        if (category) {
            countSql += ` AND c.slug = ?`;
            countParams.push(category);
        }
        if (search) {
            countSql += ` AND p.name LIKE ?`;
            countParams.push(`%${search}%`);
        }

        const { total } = db.prepare(countSql).get(...countParams);

        res.json({
            success: true,
            data: products,
            pagination: {
                page: parseInt(page),
                limit: parseInt(limit),
                total,
                pages: Math.ceil(total / limit)
            }
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

/**
 * GET /api/products/:id - ĞĞ´Ğ¸Ğ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€
 */
router.get('/:id', (req, res) => {
    try {
        const product = db.prepare(`
            SELECT p.*, c.name as category_name
            FROM products p
            LEFT JOIN categories c ON p.category_id = c.id
            WHERE p.id = ? OR p.slug = ?
        `).get(req.params.id, req.params.id);

        if (!product) {
            return res.status(404).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½'
            });
        }

        res.json({
            success: true,
            data: product
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ°:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

/**
 * GET /api/products/categories - Ğ¡Ğ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¾Ğº ĞºĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¹
 */
router.get('/categories', (req, res) => {
    try {
        const categories = db.prepare(`
            SELECT c.*, COUNT(p.id) as product_count
            FROM categories c
            LEFT JOIN products p ON p.category_id = c.id AND p.status = 'active'
            GROUP BY c.id
            ORDER BY c.sort_order, c.name
        `).all();

        res.json({
            success: true,
            data: categories
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ ĞºĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¹:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;

14.11 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 9: API Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» routes/orders.js:

const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const db = require('../models/db');
const { authenticate, optionalAuth } = require('../middleware/auth');

/**
 * POST /api/orders - Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·
 */
router.post('/', optionalAuth, (req, res) => {
    try {
        const { name, email, phone, address, comment, items } = req.body;

        // Ğ’Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ´Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
        if (!name || !email || !phone || !address) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ²ÑĞµ Ğ¾Ğ±ÑĞ·Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ñ'
            });
        }

        if (!items || items.length === 0) {
            return res.status(400).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'ĞšĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ°'
            });
        }

        // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹ Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ‘Ğ” Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ¸ Ñ†ĞµĞ½
        const productIds = items.map(i => i.id || i.product_id);
        const placeholders = productIds.map(() => '?').join(',');
        const products = db.prepare(`
            SELECT * FROM products WHERE id IN (${placeholders})
        `).all(...productIds);

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ ĞºĞ°Ñ€Ñ‚Ñƒ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²
        const productMap = {};
        products.forEach(p => productMap[p.id] = p);

        // Ğ¡Ñ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾
        let total = 0;
        const orderItems = [];

        for (const item of items) {
            const productId = item.id || item.product_id;
            const product = productMap[productId];

            if (!product) {
                return res.status(400).json({
                    success: false,
                    error: `Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€ #${productId} Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½`
                });
            }

            const itemTotal = product.price * item.quantity;
            total += itemTotal;

            orderItems.push({
                product_id: product.id,
                product_name: product.name,
                price: product.price,
                quantity: item.quantity
            });
        }

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ· Ğ² Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ·Ğ°ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸
        const createOrder = db.transaction(() => {
            // Ğ’ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·
            const orderResult = db.prepare(`
                INSERT INTO orders (user_id, name, email, phone, address, comment, total)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            `).run(
                req.user?.id || null,
                name, email, phone, address, comment || null, total
            );

            const orderId = orderResult.lastInsertRowid;

            // Ğ’ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°
            const insertItem = db.prepare(`
                INSERT INTO order_items (order_id, product_id, product_name, price, quantity)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            `);

            for (const item of orderItems) {
                insertItem.run(orderId, item.product_id, item.product_name,
                              item.price, item.quantity);
            }

            // ĞÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‰Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñƒ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½
            if (req.user) {
                db.prepare('DELETE FROM cart WHERE user_id = ?').run(req.user.id);
            }

            return orderId;
        });

        const orderId = createOrder();

        res.status(201).json({
            success: true,
            data: {
                orderId,
                total
            }
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

/**
 * GET /api/orders - Ğ—Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ñ‹ Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑƒÑ‰ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
 */
router.get('/', authenticate, (req, res) => {
    try {
        const orders = db.prepare(`
            SELECT * FROM orders
            WHERE user_id = ?
            ORDER BY created_at DESC
        `).all(req.user.id);

        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹ Ğº ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ¼Ñƒ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ñƒ
        for (const order of orders) {
            order.items = db.prepare(`
                SELECT oi.*, p.image
                FROM order_items oi
                LEFT JOIN products p ON oi.product_id = p.id
                WHERE oi.order_id = ?
            `).all(order.id);
        }

        res.json({
            success: true,
            data: orders
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²:', error);
        res.status(500).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°'
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;

14.12 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 10: Frontend â€” API ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞµĞ½Ñ‚

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» public/js/api.js:

/**
 * API ĞšĞ›Ğ˜Ğ•ĞĞ¢
 * ĞœĞ¾Ğ´ÑƒĞ»ÑŒ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ‹ Ñ REST API ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°
 */

const API = {
    baseUrl: '/api',

    /**
     * Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ´ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑĞ¾Ğ²
     */
    async request(endpoint, options = {}) {
        const url = `${this.baseUrl}${endpoint}`;

        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ ĞµÑÑ‚ÑŒ
        const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
        const headers = {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            ...options.headers
        };

        if (token) {
            headers['Authorization'] = `Bearer ${token}`;
        }

        try {
            const response = await fetch(url, {
                ...options,
                headers
            });

            const data = await response.json();

            if (!response.ok) {
                throw new Error(data.error || 'ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°');
            }

            return data;
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('API Error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    },

    // Ğ¢ĞĞ’ĞĞ Ğ«
    getProducts(params = {}) {
        const query = new URLSearchParams(params).toString();
        return this.request(`/products${query ? '?' + query : ''}`);
    },

    getProduct(id) {
        return this.request(`/products/${id}`);
    },

    getCategories() {
        return this.request('/products/categories');
    },

    // ĞšĞĞ Ğ—Ğ˜ĞĞ
    getCart() {
        return this.request('/cart');
    },

    addToCart(productId, quantity = 1) {
        return this.request('/cart/add', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify({ productId, quantity })
        });
    },

    removeFromCart(productId) {
        return this.request(`/cart/remove/${productId}`, {
            method: 'DELETE'
        });
    },

    // Ğ—ĞĞšĞĞ—Ğ«
    createOrder(orderData) {
        return this.request('/orders', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify(orderData)
        });
    },

    getOrders() {
        return this.request('/orders');
    },

    // ĞĞ’Ğ¢ĞĞ Ğ˜Ğ—ĞĞ¦Ğ˜Ğ¯
    register(data) {
        return this.request('/auth/register', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify(data)
        });
    },

    login(email, password) {
        return this.request('/auth/login', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })
        });
    },

    getCurrentUser() {
        return this.request('/auth/me');
    }
};

window.API = API;

14.13 Ğ¨Ğ°Ğ³ 11: Frontend â€” ĞšĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°

Ğ¤Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ» public/js/cart.js:

/**
 * ĞœĞĞ”Ğ£Ğ›Ğ¬ ĞšĞĞ Ğ—Ğ˜ĞĞ«
 * Ğ Ğ°Ğ±Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ Ñ localStorage Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ³Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¹ Ğ¸ Ñ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…
 */

const Cart = {
    items: [],
    isAuthenticated: false,

    /**
     * Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ° ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‹
     */
    async load() {
        if (this.isAuthenticated) {
            try {
                const response = await API.getCart();
                this.items = response.data || [];
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ÑƒĞ·ĞºĞ¸ ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‹:', error);
                this.items = [];
            }
        } else {
            // Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ğ³Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¹ â€” Ğ¸Ğ· localStorage
            this.items = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cart')) || [];
        }
        this.updateUI();
    },

    /**
     * Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€
     */
    async add(product) {
        if (this.isAuthenticated) {
            try {
                await API.addToCart(product.id);
                await this.load();
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ:', error);
            }
        } else {
            // Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ğ³Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¹ â€” Ğ² localStorage
            const existing = this.items.find(i => i.id === product.id);

            if (existing) {
                existing.quantity++;
            } else {
                this.items.push({
                    id: product.id,
                    name: product.name,
                    price: product.price,
                    image: product.image,
                    quantity: 1
                });
            }

            this.save();
        }

        Toast.show(`${product.name} Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½ Ğ² ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñƒ`, 'success');
    },

    /**
     * Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€
     */
    async remove(productId) {
        if (this.isAuthenticated) {
            await API.removeFromCart(productId);
            await this.load();
        } else {
            this.items = this.items.filter(i => i.id !== productId);
            this.save();
        }
    },

    /**
     * Ğ˜Ğ·Ğ¼ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ĞºĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾
     */
    updateQuantity(productId, quantity) {
        const item = this.items.find(i => i.id === productId);
        if (item) {
            item.quantity = Math.max(1, quantity);
            this.save();
        }
    },

    /**
     * Ğ¡Ğ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ² localStorage
     */
    save() {
        localStorage.setItem('cart', JSON.stringify(this.items));
        this.updateUI();
    },

    /**
     * ĞÑ‡Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñƒ
     */
    clear() {
        this.items = [];
        localStorage.removeItem('cart');
        this.updateUI();
    },

    /**
     * ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾
     */
    getTotal() {
        return this.items.reduce((sum, item) => {
            return sum + item.price * item.quantity;
        }, 0);
    },

    /**
     * ĞšĞ¾Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¾ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²
     */
    getCount() {
        return this.items.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.quantity, 0);
    },

    /**
     * ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ UI (ÑÑ‡Ñ‘Ñ‚Ñ‡Ğ¸Ğº Ğ² ÑˆĞ°Ğ¿ĞºĞµ)
     */
    updateUI() {
        const counter = document.getElementById('cart-count');
        if (counter) {
            const count = this.getCount();
            counter.textContent = count;
            counter.style.display = count > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
        }
    },

    /**
     * Ğ¡Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ…Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ ĞºĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ‹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ Ğ²Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´Ğµ
     */
    async syncWithServer() {
        if (this.items.length > 0) {
            try {
                await API.syncCart(this.items);
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('ĞÑˆĞ¸Ğ±ĞºĞ° ÑĞ¸Ğ½Ñ…Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸:', error);
            }
        }
        await this.load();
    }
};

/**
 * Ğ£Ğ²ĞµĞ´Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ (Toast)
 */
const Toast = {
    show(message, type = 'info') {
        let container = document.getElementById('toast-container');
        if (!container) {
            container = document.createElement('div');
            container.id = 'toast-container';
            container.className = 'toast-container';
            document.body.appendChild(container);
        }

        const toast = document.createElement('div');
        toast.className = `toast ${type}`;
        toast.textContent = message;
        container.appendChild(toast);

        setTimeout(() => toast.remove(), 3000);
    }
};

window.Cart = Cart;
window.Toast = Toast;

15.4 Ğ‘Ğ°Ğ·Ğ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… SQLite

Ğ”Ğ»Ñ Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ñ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¼ Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ° Ğ±Ğ°Ğ·Ğ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…. SQLite â€” Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ Ğ‘Ğ”, Ğ½Ğµ Ñ‚Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒÑÑ‰Ğ°Ñ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ´ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ°.

// npm install better-sqlite3

const Database = require('better-sqlite3');
const db = new Database('shop.db');

// Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ñ‚Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¸Ñ†Ñ‹
db.exec(`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS products (
        id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
        name TEXT NOT NULL,
        price REAL NOT NULL,
        stock INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
    )
`);

// Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… (INSERT)

    INSERT INTO products (name, price, stock)
    VALUES (?, ?, ?)
`);

const products = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM products').all();

// Ğ£Ğ´Ğ°Ğ»ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ (DELETE)
db.prepare('DELETE FROM products WHERE id = ?').run(1);

ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾ÑÑ‹ â€” Ğ·Ğ°Ñ‰Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚ SQL-Ğ¸Ğ½ÑŠĞµĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¹

ğŸ’¡ Ğ¢Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ·Ğ°ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ â€” Ğ°Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¾Ğ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

ĞšĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ½ÑƒĞ¶Ğ½Ğ¾ Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑŒ Ğ½ĞµÑĞºĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞºĞ¾ ÑĞ²ÑĞ·Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ… Ğ¾Ğ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¹, Ğ¸ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·ÑƒĞ¹Ñ‚Ğµ Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ·Ğ°ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸. Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¾Ğ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ Ğ¿Ğ°Ğ´Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ â€” Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ°Ñ‚Ñ‹Ğ²Ğ°ÑÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ²ÑĞµ.

const createOrder = db.transaction((items) => {
    // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·
    const order = db.prepare('INSERT INTO orders...').run();

    // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

        db.prepare('INSERT INTO order_items...').run(item);
        db.prepare('UPDATE products SET stock = stock - ?...').run(item.qty);

    return order.lastInsertRowid;
});

// Ğ•ÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ñ‡Ñ‚Ğ¾-Ñ‚Ğ¾ ÑƒĞ¿Ğ°Ğ´Ñ‘Ñ‚ â€” Ğ²ÑÑ‘ Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºĞ°Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ‚ÑÑ

15.5 JWT-Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ

JWT (JSON Web Token) â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ğ½Ğ´Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‚ Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ±ĞµĞ·Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ°ÑĞ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€ĞµĞ´Ğ°Ñ‡Ğ¸ Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ ĞºĞ»Ğ¸ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ¸ ÑĞµÑ€Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¼.

// npm install jsonwebtoken bcryptjs

const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');

const JWT_SECRET = 'Ğ²Ğ°Ñˆ-ÑĞµĞºÑ€ĞµÑ‚Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹-ĞºĞ»ÑÑ‡';

// Ğ ĞµĞ³Ğ¸ÑÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
app.post('/api/auth/register', async (req, res) => {
    const { email, password, name } = req.body;

    // Ğ¥ĞµÑˆĞ¸Ñ€ÑƒĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ (Ğ½Ğ¸ĞºĞ¾Ğ³Ğ´Ğ° Ğ½Ğµ Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¾!)
    const hashedPassword = bcrypt.hashSync(password, 10);

    // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
    const result = db.prepare(`
        INSERT INTO users (email, password, name)
        VALUES (?, ?, ?)
    `).run(email, hashedPassword, name);

    // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½
    const token = jwt.sign(
        { userId: result.lastInsertRowid },
        JWT_SECRET,
        { expiresIn: '7d' }
    );

    res.json({ success: true, token });
});

// Ğ’Ñ…Ğ¾Ğ´
app.post('/api/auth/login', (req, res) => {
    const { email, password } = req.body;

    const user = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM users WHERE email = ?').get(email);

    if (!user || !bcrypt.compareSync(password, user.password)) {
        return res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞĞµĞ²ĞµÑ€Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ email Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒ'
        });
    }

    const token = jwt.sign({ userId: user.id }, JWT_SECRET, { expiresIn: '7d' });

    res.json({ success: true, token, user: { id: user.id, name: user.name } });
});

Middleware Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ¸ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸

// middleware/auth.js
function authenticate(req, res, next) {
    // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½ Ğ¸Ğ· Ğ·Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ°
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;

    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
        return res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'Ğ¢Ñ€ĞµĞ±ÑƒĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ°Ğ²Ñ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ'
        });
    }

    const token = authHeader.split(' ')[1];

    try {
        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½
        const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);

        // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑƒÑ‡Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ
        const user = db.prepare('SELECT id, email, name, role FROM users WHERE id = ?')
            .get(decoded.userId);

        if (!user) {
            return res.status(401).json({
                success: false,
                error: 'ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½'
            });
        }

        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ»Ñ Ğ² Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ
        req.user = user;
        next();
    } catch (error) {
        return res.status(401).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞĞµĞ´ĞµĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞ»ÑŒĞ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ñ‚Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½'
        });
    }
}

// Ğ˜ÑĞ¿Ğ¾Ğ»ÑŒĞ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ
app.get('/api/orders', authenticate, (req, res) => {
    // req.user Ğ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½ Ğ±Ğ»Ğ°Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ°Ñ€Ñ middleware
    const orders = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM orders WHERE user_id = ?')
        .all(req.user.id);
    res.json({ success: true, data: orders });
});
âš ï¸ Ğ‘ĞµĞ·Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ°ÑĞ½Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑŒ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»ĞµĞ¹:
  • ĞĞ˜ĞšĞĞ“Ğ”Ğ Ğ½Ğµ Ñ…Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğµ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ² Ğ¾Ñ‚ĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ¼ Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ´Ğµ

  • Ğ¢Ğ¾ĞºĞµĞ½Ñ‹ Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¶Ğ½Ñ‹ Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ‚ÑŒ ÑÑ€Ğ¾Ğº Ğ´ĞµĞ¹ÑÑ‚Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ (expiresIn)

15.6 ĞŸĞ¾Ğ»Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¼ĞµÑ€: API Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ³Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°

Ğ¡Ğ¾ĞµĞ´Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ²ÑÑ‘ Ğ²Ğ¼ĞµÑÑ‚Ğµ Ğ¸ ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ¼ API Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ½Ğ°ÑˆĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ğ¼Ğ°Ğ³Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°:

// routes/products.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const db = require('../models/db');

// GET /api/products â€” ÑĞ¿Ğ¸ÑĞ¾Ğº Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ² Ñ Ñ„Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒÑ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸ĞµĞ¹
router.get('/', (req, res) => {
    const { category, search, sort = 'created_at', order = 'desc', page = 1, limit = 12 } = req.query;

    let sql = `
        SELECT p.*, c.name as category_name
        FROM products p
        LEFT JOIN categories c ON p.category_id = c.id
        WHERE p.status = 'active'
    `;
    const params = [];

    // Ğ¤Ğ¸Ğ»ÑŒÑ‚Ñ€ Ğ¿Ğ¾ ĞºĞ°Ñ‚ĞµĞ³Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ¸
    if (category) {
        sql += ' AND c.slug = ?';
        params.push(category);
    }

    // ĞŸĞ¾Ğ¸ÑĞº
    if (search) {
        sql += ' AND p.name LIKE ?';
        params.push(`%${search}%`);
    }

    // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ñ€Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞºĞ°
    const allowedSort = ['name', 'price', 'created_at'];
    const sortField = allowedSort.includes(sort) ? sort : 'created_at';
    sql += ` ORDER BY p.${sortField} ${order === 'asc' ? 'ASC' : 'DESC'}`;

    // ĞŸĞ°Ğ³Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ
    const offset = (page - 1) * limit;
    sql += ` LIMIT ? OFFSET ?`;
    params.push(parseInt(limit), offset);

    const products = db.prepare(sql).all(...params);

    res.json({ success: true, data: products });
});

// GET /api/products/:id â€” Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ¸Ğ½ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€
router.get('/:id', (req, res) => {
    const product = db.prepare(`
        SELECT * FROM products WHERE id = ? OR slug = ?
    `).get(req.params.id, req.params.id);

    if (!product) {
        return res.status(404).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ½Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ´ĞµĞ½'
        });
    }

    res.json({ success: true, data: product });
});

module.exports = router;

// routes/orders.js
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const db = require('../models/db');
const { authenticate } = require('../middleware/auth');

// POST /api/orders â€” ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·Ğ°
router.post('/', authenticate, (req, res) => {
    const { name, email, phone, address, items } = req.body;

    // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ĞºĞ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ñ…
    if (!items || items.length === 0) {
        return res.status(400).json({
            success: false,
            error: 'ĞšĞ¾Ñ€Ğ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ° Ğ¿ÑƒÑÑ‚Ğ°'
        });
    }

    // Ğ¢Ñ€Ğ°Ğ½Ğ·Ğ°ĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ñ â€” Ğ²ÑÑ‘ Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸ Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ‡ĞµĞ³Ğ¾
    const createOrder = db.transaction(() => {
        let total = 0;

        // ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞµĞ¼ Ñ‚Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€Ñ‹ Ğ¸ ÑÑ‡Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ°ĞµĞ¼ ÑÑƒĞ¼Ğ¼Ñƒ
        for (const item of items) {
            const product = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM products WHERE id = ?')
                .get(item.id);

            if (!product || product.stock < item.quantity) {
                throw new Error(`Ğ¢Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ñ€ ${product?.name || item.id} Ğ½ĞµĞ´Ğ¾ÑÑ‚ÑƒĞ¿ĞµĞ½`);
            }

            total += product.price * item.quantity;
        }

        // Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‘Ğ¼ Ğ·Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ·
        const result = db.prepare(`
            INSERT INTO orders (user_id, total, name, email, phone, address)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
        `).run(req.user.id, total, name, email, phone, address);

        const orderId = result.lastInsertRowid;

        // Ğ”Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ»ÑĞµĞ¼ Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ·Ğ¸Ñ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¸ ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½ÑŒÑˆĞ°ĞµĞ¼ Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‚ĞºĞ¸
        for (const item of items) {
            const product = db.prepare('SELECT * FROM products WHERE id = ?')
                .get(item.id);

            db.prepare(`
                INSERT INTO order_items (order_id, product_id, product_name, price, quantity)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            `).run(orderId, product.id, product.name, product.price, item.quantity);

            db.prepare('UPDATE products SET stock = stock - ? WHERE id = ?')
                .run(item.quantity, product.id);
        }

        return orderId;
    });

    try {
        const orderId = createOrder();
        res.status(201).json({
            success: true,
            message: 'Ğ—Ğ°ĞºĞ°Ğ· ÑĞ¾Ğ·Ğ´Ğ°Ğ½',
            data: { orderId }
        });
    } catch (error) {
        res.status(400).json({
            success: false,
            error: error.message
        });
    }
});

module.exports = router;
